      *    *COMPUTE (x1 / x2 * x3)
      * x1    : DB1.Quantity Ordered
      * /     : PGM.*Synon (15,2) work field *Rounded
      * x2    : LCL.Number Cases On A Pallet
      * *     : PGM.*Synon (15,2) work field *Rounded
      * x3    : LCL.Pallet Tare Weight
     C           TBAVQT    DIV  YL0146    W0WA01    H      *Synon (15,2) w
     C           W0WA01    MULT YL0147    W0WA00    H      *Synon (15,2) w
     C                     Z-ADDW0WA00    YL0151           Weight 1.2
     C                     ELSE
      * CASE: *OTHERWISE
     C                     Z-ADD*ZERO     YL0151           Weight 1.2
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     ELSE
      * CASE: *OTHERWISE
     C                     Z-ADD*ZERO     YL0151           Weight 1.2
     C                     END                             *FI
      * Estimated Gross
      * DB1.OD Minimum Unit Weight =
      *    *COMPUTE (x1 + x2 + x3)
      * x1    : DB1.Weight Ordered
      * +     : PGM.*Synon (15,2) work field
      * x2    : LCL.Weight 1.1             .U
      * +     : PGM.*Synon (15,2) work field
      * x3    : LCL.Weight 1.2             .U
     C           TBD0WG    ADD  YL0150    W0WA01           *Synon (15,2) w
     C           W0WA01    ADD  YL0151    W0WA00           *Synon (15,2) w
     C                     Z-ADDW0WA00    TBH8NX           OD Estimated Gr
      * E00196 RMC 8/24/12 chk pfs interface SHPTRN too
      *================================================================
